(3) Xi Qiran, a preparatory committee member of the 32nd Division of the Army Special Party Department, resigned; Wang Qinghan was appointed to replace him; (4) Chen Yunkui, a preparatory committee member of the newly编制的 34th Division of the Army Special Party Department, was vacant due to illness; Xi Renjie was appointed to replace him; (5) The "Measures for Assessing the Training Performance of Provisional Party Members in Military Special Party Departments" were approved; (6) The "Measures for Raising Overseas Chinese Education Funds," "Measures for Donating and Rewarding Overseas Chinese Education Funds," and "Organizational Regulations for the Overseas Chinese Education Fund Management Committee" were approved; (7) Zuo Gong, director of the Censorship Department of the Central Propaganda Department, resigned due to illness; the resignation was approved; (8) Committee Member Wu Jingheng was nominated to deliver a report at next Monday's Central Commemoration Week.

Central Committee Holds Memorial Service for Liao Zhongkai's Martyrdom 74

The Central Party Headquarters held a memorial service today (the 20th) to commemorate the sixth anniversary of Liao Zhongkai's martyrdom. Attendees included Zhu Jiahua, Jiao Yitang, Fang Juehui, Zhou Qigang, Yu Youren, Ding Weifen, Wang Boqun, Wu Zhihui, Cai Yuanpei, Miao Peicheng, Chen Zhaoying, Chen Lifu, Shao Yuanchong, as well as staff and guests, totaling approximately 600 people. The memorial ceremony included (1) Standing at attention as a whole; (2) Singing the Party Song; (3) Bowing three times to the portraits of the Premier and Mr. Liao; (4) Observing three minutes of silence; (5) The Chairman delivering the opening remarks; (6) Speeches; (7) Conclusion. Chairman Fang Juehui delivered a speech, stating in brief: "Our annual commemoration of the martyr Mr. Liao must have far-reaching significance and value. Mr. Liao was a very revolutionary member of our party. During the Republic of China era, the party became corrupt. Mr. Liao helped the Premier reorganize the Chinese Revolutionary Party. In 1917, some corrupt members of the party colluded with the Political Studies Clique to oppose the Premier. Mr. Liao followed the Premier to Shanghai to publish the Construction Magazine. In 1922, Mr. Liao had a plan to unify military and financial affairs. In 1924, he assisted the Premier in reorganizing the Kuomintang, revitalizing its spirit, and founding the Whampoa Military Academy. The current Chairman Chiang serves as the principal, and the party representative was Mr. Liao. His spirit was demonstrated by personally engaging in mass work in his capacity as a minister. Today, we should commemorate Mr. Liao's spirit and the greatness of his revolutionary personality. Mr. Liao managed the finances for several years but ended up with nothing. This is the value of Mr. Liao that is worth commemorating," etc. Next, Wu Zhihui delivered a speech, stating in brief: "On August 20, 1925, Mr. Liao was martyred, and the party lost a useful talent. The eight characters in our Party Song, 'Swear to be diligent and brave, and must be faithful and loyal,' can be applied to Mr. Liao without any embarrassment. Mr. Liao also had the ability to build. It is a pity that he sacrificed himself while he was struggling. Our annual commemoration is like getting a shot of morphine. Even if it is only five minutes of heat, it should be exciting. I hope everyone will learn from the virtues of the martyrs. Confucius said, 'If one does not violate benevolence for three months, one may be considered benevolent.' The meaning of our commemoration lies in this." Subsequently, the conclusion of the ceremony was announced, and the meeting was adjourned.

Dangerous Situation on the Yellow River Near Jinan 75

▲ Stone Dam at Luokou Collapses by Several Zhang (Units of Length)

▲ Only Forty Li (Units of Length) from Jinan

▲ Yellow River Water Rises Above the Danger Line

Jinan Correspondence: The Yellow River's water level rose another three inches last night (the 18th). The Luokou water gauge north of the city has reached a height of nine zhang three chi one cun above sea level, exceeding the danger line by one cun. The entire riverbank feels increasingly dangerous. Zhang Lianjia, director of the River Affairs Bureau, immediately set out to supervise the emergency repairs. However, shortly after arriving at Luokou, the North Diansi in Changqing County, thirty li northwest of Luokou on the south bank, experienced a dangerous situation as several zhang of the stone dam collapsed. The area is only forty li from Jinan and is of critical importance. In case of an accident, Jinan's low-lying terrain would be unimaginable. Zhang Lianjia convened an urgent meeting that evening in Luokou, attended by the district heads of the ninth and tenth districts of Jinan City, the director of the Luokou Public Security Bureau, and the staff of various sections of the midstream. They planned emergency repairs. It is noted that North Diansi has historically had the fewest dangerous sections in the midstream of the Yellow River in Shandong Province and has the most solid stone dam. Now that even it has experienced a dangerous situation, the danger in the upstream and downstream areas, which are riddled with holes and historically have many dangerous sections, can be imagined. (19th)

Another Telegram: The Yellow River's water level is rising rapidly, and telegrams reporting emergencies upstream and downstream are arriving like snowflakes. The Tangjia in Huimin and the Sunjia in Lijin on the north bank downstream, the Wangwangzhuang in Putai on the south bank, and the Miannian in Kangtun and the Liu Zhuang Zhukou in Puyang County and the Miannian in Liuyuan on the north bank upstream are all extremely dangerous. Shandong Provincial Chairman Han Fuju has telegraphed the public security bureau chiefs and county magistrates of the twenty-two counties along the river and the director of the River Affairs Bureau, Zhang Lianjia, ordering them to go to the worksite immediately to supervise and order emergency repairs. According to a person from the River Affairs Bureau, when the Gongjia Dam breached ten years ago, the Luokou water gauge was only nine zhang five chi. Now, it has been found that the water that rose three chi four cun six fen two li in Shaanxi on the 17th has not yet reached Jinan. The water level in Shandong Province has already reached nine zhang two chi eight cun. If that water arrives, it will definitely rise to more than nine zhang five chi, and there is a risk of a breach. All the staff of the River Affairs Bureau have been working day and night since the 17th, extremely busy. Due to continuous heavy rain, the autumn crops in Liaocheng in western Shandong have been submerged, resulting in a flood. As of the 15th, it was still raining non-stop. Suddenly, it was reported that the Tuhai River south of the city had breached by several zhang, and the area near the city walls had become a swamp. The 87th Brigade Commander Rong Guangxing, upon hearing the news, immediately led more than 2,000 officers and soldiers stationed in Liaocheng to rush to the emergency repairs. At the time, it was raining heavily, and the water was surging. Finally, thanks to the valiant efforts of the officers and soldiers, the repairs were completed by 6:00 PM. Fortunately, it was successful. (18th)

Lu Han Temporarily Postpones Trip to Peiping 76

▲ Reason is Reorganization of the Shi Department

▲ The Shi Department Will Be Temporarily Organized into a Brigade

▲ Han's Troops Deployed to Attack Liu's Department

Jinan Correspondence: Since the Shi Yousan Department was resolved, Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang, in response to the aftermath of the situation in North China, summoned generals from all parties to consult. He recently invited Shandong Provincial Chairman Han Fuju to Peiping. Today, a reporter visited Han and asked if the travel date had been set. Han said that he could not go to Peiping temporarily due to the reorganization of the Shi Department. If there were important events in the future, he might have to go to Peiping. As for the reorganization of the Shi Department, because it originally had only more than 5,000 people, it could not be organized into a division. Therefore, it was planned to incorporate it into the Zhan Shutang Department and expand the Zhan Brigade into the 73rd Division, with Zhan being promoted to division commander. According to news from the headquarters today, after several consultations on the reorganization of the Shi Department, it has now been decided to reorganize it into a temporary brigade based on the current number of personnel, with Shi's chief of staff, Tang Bangzhi, appointed as the brigade commander. The number has not yet been determined. Once the reorganization is complete, it will remain in Jinan for training. It is noted that the Shi Department, which surrendered to Lu, has successively arrived in Jinan in full from Yucheng as of yesterday (the 17th) and should be able to begin reorganization within days. Also, according to news here, there are still more than a thousand people in the Shi Department in Hebei Province who wanted to surrender to Lu and be absorbed. While traveling to the northwest of Zaoqiang County, they were intercepted by the Northeast Army and completely resolved, preventing them from coming south.

Han Fuju's representative, Song Shiyan, previously accompanied Deputy Zhang's representatives, Fan Pujiang and Ge Guangting, to Peiping to meet Zhang and report on the progress of the reorganization of the Shi Department. Today, Song returned to Jinan from Peiping. According to reports, the Deputy Commander fully agreed with Chairman Han's absorption and reorganization of the Shi Department. The overall situation in North China is calm.

As always, the generals of the Northwest Army and the Jin Army unanimously support the Central Government and will not be affected by Yan's return to Jin. The Deputy Commander is very willing to work with Chairman Han to maintain the overall situation in the North.

Han Fuju recently received orders to send troops to resolve the Liu Guitang Department in Daming. He ordered the 29th Division Commander Cao Fulin to command the Li Hanzhang Brigade and the Li Xuande Cavalry Brigade to take the road through En County, Xiajin, and Weixian to Daming. Today, Li Hanzhang returned to Dezhou from Jinan to defend the border. According to Li, he was ordered to go to Daming to attack the Liu Guitang Department but was unable to bear the heavy responsibility due to illness. Chairman Han has now reassigned the Chen Dexin Department of the 86th Brigade to go, still under the command of Division Commander Cao, along with the Cavalry Brigade, Li Xuande. A heavy mortar company from the 29th Division was also transferred from Dezhou to join them. They arrived in Pingyuan today and will be mobilized tomorrow (the 19th), taking the road through Guantao to Daming. It is said that the Li Xuande Department will be mobilized today. Division Commander Cao is still in Yucheng. The Liu Guitang Department in Daming City has about a thousand people and intends to hold their ground. (August 18)

Continued Reports on the Tragic Murder of Jinan Female Teacher Zhu Shude 77

▲ Wang and Zhu Definitely Had a Relationship

Jinan Correspondence: Shandong Provincial Chairman Han Fuju spoke today (the 18th) on the suicide case of Zhu Shude, a teacher at the Second Provincial Elementary School of Shandong. The reason for Zhu Shude's suicide has now been clarified. It has been confirmed that Zhu Shude and Wang Weijun had a relationship. Because she suffered great pain as a result of the relationship, she committed suicide. Therefore, Wang Weijun is ultimately responsible. Wang is the section chief of the Education Department and has now been suspended from his duties. This case is different from that of Bai Wan, where heroin was involved; it should be resolved by law.

Yesterday (the 17th) was Sunday, and the court was not open for business. However, a special investigative court was convened for the Zhu case, with Chief Prosecutor Li in attendance. Only Wang Weijun's female servant, Chen Wangshi, was interrogated. Her testimony was largely the same as before: (1) There is a handgun in Wang Weijun's home, which she had seen before; (2) Wang Weijun and Zhu Shude had a relationship and had cohabited, which is true. As for whether she had given birth to a child, she did not know; (3) The affairs of the Wang family were known to almost all the neighbors. Based on Chen Wangshi's testimony, the court convened another investigative court today and specially summoned Wang Weijun's neighbors to inquire about Wang and Zhu's relationship. The neighbors testified that they did not know. When asked whether the Wang family's female servant testified that the neighbors knew about it, they replied that they heard about the Wang family having a handgun but did not know anything else. The court immediately adjourned. Wu Zhen, president of the High Court, went to the Provincial Public Security Bureau this morning to consult the household registration register and confirmed that Wang Weijun did indeed cohabit with Zhu Shude at No. 31 Xiaowangfu Street between July and August of last year. The name on the household registration register was Wang Shiheng.

According to Zhu Meirong, a relative of Zhu Shude, when the court opened on the 15th, she wanted to describe in detail Wang Weijun's seduction of Zhu Shude and their cohabitation on Xiaowangfu Street, but the judge did not allow her to speak, and she did not know why. It was discovered that Wang Weijun had formally married Zhu Shude in Qingdao when the Jin Army arrived in Jinan last year. After returning to Jinan, Shude became pregnant, and Liu Hesheng (Wang's wife) became jealous and did not allow Zhu to cohabit with Wang at the Wang residence. She moved to No. 31 Xiaowangfu Street (the newly replaced porcelain door number 30) to live. After I found out, I personally visited the place and was told by her female servant that it was Wang's mansion and refused to see me. Later, I wrote a letter in my own hand, addressed to Mrs. Wang, Shude to receive, and was able to see Zhu Shude. On the small building in the courtyard, she told me about being seduced by Wang Weijun. It has now been discovered that Wang Weijun changed his name to Wang Shiheng (serving as a section chief in the Education Department) when he registered his household in Xiaowangfu Street, and the wife was Zhu. Since it was registered as wife Zhu, it shows that he had married Zhu Shude. Also, Education Department Director He Siyuan said that at the beginning of this case, the court came to the scene to inspect and found that the deceased was indeed a virgin and had no relationship with Wang Weijun. Wang was a recommended official, so the Education Department did not suspend him from his duties that day. Now that the court has detained him to investigate his relationship with this case, the Education Department also suspended him from his position as section chief yesterday, pending a legal resolution. Also, according to news from the court, this case will be prosecuted. After many days of investigation, it has been determined that Zhu Shude did commit suicide, and her suicide note has been proven to be in her own handwriting and is not a forgery.

Zhu Shude's Posthumous Portrait 78

I was known to him after I visited his friends on behalf of Zhu Shude.

Minutes of the Second Jiangsu Provincial Congress 79

▲ Passed a proposal to revitalize the province's politics

▲ And determined six articles of administrative and operational methods

Yesterday (the 20th) was the sixth day of the Second Jiangsu Provincial Congress. At 8 a.m., a memorial service for Liao Zhongkai was held, attended by 89 representatives. The presidium nominated Huang Yuren as chairman, who led the ceremony. The chairman reported, stating briefly that the gathering of representatives from all counties of the province to commemorate Mr. Liao had even greater significance. First, Mr. Liao was targeted and attacked by reactionaries for advocating the unification of military, civil, and financial administration. However, in today's China, these three have not been unified. We should continue his legacy and complete this important mission. Second, Mr. Liao consistently supported and upheld the party. Today, the party affairs in Jiangsu are disorganized, the discipline is lax, and the strength is weak. We should follow Mr. Liao's spirit of hard work, focus our efforts on party affairs in the province, enforce strict discipline, and strengthen the organization. Third, Mr. Liao served as the Minister of Agriculture and Labor and paid close attention to the lives of farmers and workers. We should emulate him and carry out practical work in the mass movement. The ceremony concluded at 9 a.m., followed by the fourth general assembly, chaired by Huang Yuren. First, the minutes of the previous meeting were read. Xu Wenjun, the representative of the proposal review committee, reported that 92 proposals were received yesterday, combining with over 200 existing ones, and very few have been resolved. A faster method of discussion is needed. Next, the proposals were discussed: (1) Proposal to revitalize the province's politics (submitted by the Provincial Party Rectification Committee). Ma Yinbing first gave a detailed explanation, including promoting local autonomy, rectifying officialdom, eliminating accumulated land tax malpractices, improving the judiciary, and improving education. Representatives Wang Zhongjun, Jiang Yanqiu, Luo Decheng, Huang Songtao, Cai Peifu, Zhao Yuzheng, Tang Kesheng, Liu Jian, Xi Hanping, Xin Yutang, Zhuang Minqiu, Qiu Youling, Wang Gongyu, Ge Jianshi, Ma Wenzao, etc., expressed their opinions. As a result of the discussion, all opinions were submitted to another review committee for review. The review committee consisted of seven members, with a double number of candidates introduced by the presidium. The following were elected by all representatives: Liu Jian, Wang Gongyu, Qiu Youzhen, Ma Wenzao, Peng Liren, Xin Yutang, Peng Binghou, with Liu Jian designated as convener. (2) Request for the Provincial Government to set a deadline for reducing the number of police teams in each county and to organize local defense groups in each township and district (submitted by representatives from Gaochun, etc.). (3) Proposal to increase the powers of county magistrates to facilitate county administration and accountability (submitted by representatives from Wujin, etc.). (4) Proposal to complete the land survey in the province as soon as possible to realize the Principle of People's Livelihood (submitted by representatives from Jiangning, etc.). (5) Proposal to divide the stages and set a deadline for completing county autonomy to realize provincial autonomy (submitted by representatives from Fengxian, etc.). (6) Proposal to abolish the public security mu tax to reduce the burden on farmers (submitted by representatives from Jiangning, etc.). It was resolved that the above six proposals be combined and submitted to the review committee for the proposal to revitalize the province's politics for review. (7) Proposal to temporarily suspend the police academy (submitted by representatives from Jiangyin, etc.). After the proposal was put forward, the representatives debated fiercely whether to approve it. As it was past 12 o'clock, many representatives requested to postpone the discussion until the afternoon. The chairman then announced the adjournment.

At 2 p.m., the fifth general assembly was held, chaired by Huang Yuren, with 77 representatives present. The discussion continued: (1) Proposal to temporarily suspend the police academy. It was resolved to pass it according to the review opinion. Attached review opinion: It is natural to run a police academy, but the management is not perfect. The Civil Affairs Department should thoroughly rectify it. The training of police students and the issue of employment after graduation should be planned and handled by the Civil Affairs Department. (3) Suggest that the Central Government consult the National Government to promulgate the New Salt Law within this year (submitted by representatives from Qidong, etc.). It was resolved to pass it. (3) Suggest that the Central Government build the southernmost section of the coastline as soon as possible to facilitate transportation and enrich people's livelihood (submitted by representatives from Qidong, etc.). It was resolved that the Provincial Executive Committee should request the Ministry of Railways to complete the construction before the 21st year. (4) Consult the Jiangsu Provincial Government to allocate funds to dredge Chishan Lake to benefit farmland and avoid drought and flood (submitted by representatives from Jurong, etc.). It was resolved to send a letter to the Jiangsu Provincial Government, ordering the Department of Construction to send personnel to conduct on-site surveys, draft a dredging plan, and start construction within the year. The required funds should be used from the water conservancy funds collected from the three counties of Jiang, Ju, and Li. (5) The internal river navigation rights of the China Merchants Bureau in this province should be taken over and managed by this province, and it should be determined that all income from this case should be used for the development of agriculture and hydropower in various counties (submitted by representatives from Jiangyin, etc.). It was resolved to retain it. (6) Rickshaws in each county should be taken over by the local government to increase local revenue and relieve the suffering of rickshaw pullers (submitted by representatives from Wujin, etc.). It was resolved to withdraw this case. (7) The provincial and county road construction in this province should be paid for and exempted from taxes at any time when using civilian land (submitted by representatives from Jiangyin, etc.). It was resolved to pass it. (8) The Department of Construction cannot be responsible for the repair and management of the Jiangbei Canal, resulting in an unprecedented disaster. Now, six articles of follow-up measures are proposed for public decision to avoid another disaster (submitted by Gu Tingcong from Xinghua, etc.). It was resolved to pass it. Measures: 1. The canal project should be managed by an independent agency for flexible command. Its name may be restored to the old system or changed to the Jiangbei Canal Water Conservancy Bureau. 2. The position of the director should be raised, and a person familiar with river affairs should be appointed by the Central Government. 3. The relevant counties may elect representatives to form a council and a supervisory committee to participate in the design. 4. The mu tax for governance and operation paid by the 25 counties should be stored in a special account and not be used without the consent of the council. 5. The counties in the east of the canal are the tail end of the Huai River. Before there is a practical solution to guide the Huai River, in order to maintain the lives and property of tens of millions of people in the downstream dozens of counties, the provincial government should request the central government to allocate 5 million yuan for the governance of the canal and ports. 6. After this case is passed, consult the provincial government to be responsible for implementation within two months. (9) Please ask the Central Government to formulate a concrete plan for equalizing land rights, implement it within a time limit to stabilize society, and stabilize the political foundation (submitted by representatives from Wuxi, etc.). It was resolved to pass it. (10) Reduce the burden on students and set up free and scholarship quotas (submitted by representatives from Zhenjiang, etc.). It was resolved to pass it. Measures: 1. Reduce tuition fees and do not collect improper fees under various pretexts. 2. All levels of schools should set up more free and scholarship quotas. 3. Raise a fund for poor education to subsidize outstanding children from poor families to go to school. 4. Establish a method for selecting outstanding children from poor families. 5. Children of current primary and secondary school teachers should be exempt from tuition fees. (11) Please order the party departments of each county that anyone who has hosted anti-Japanese meetings in the past, has had fraudulent circumstances, or has not handled matters well and has not settled accounts

Page 12

to be uniformly prohibited from participating in this anti-Japanese meeting (submitted by representatives from Shanghai, etc.). It was resolved to pass it. (12) Severely punish local bullies and evil gentry to prevent the growth of feudal forces and benefit the promotion of party affairs. It was resolved to submit all opinions to the review committee for re-examination. Temporary motions: (1) Please transfer the banquet fees for the reception of representatives from various agencies to be used as flood relief publicity fees. It was resolved to pass it. (2) Please schedule a visit to the mausoleum of the Prime Minister. It was resolved to pass it, and the date will be determined by the presidium.

Urgent News from Wuhu 80

▲ Wuhu is suffering from a major flood, and the embankments have been successively breached and exhausted. The only remaining one is the Wanchun embankment. Unexpectedly, at 10 p.m. last night, several feet of the gate of the embankment suddenly collapsed, causing another risk. However, when the risk occurred, gunshots were suddenly heard at the scene, which may have been caused by bandits. County Magistrate Yu has led a team to investigate.

▲ The Shanghai Bank of China entrusted the Wuhu branch to investigate the disaster situation in Wuhu. The general situation found has been replied by letter yesterday. The main points are that Wuhu has a total of more than 500,000 mu of embanked fields, and now only the Wanchun Township Special Zone has less than 60,000 mu of embanked fields. There are about 240,000 disaster victims in the township area and 100,000 in the urban area. There are even more refugees fleeing to Wuhu from nearby areas. The current emergency relief, that is, food and housing, is not enough without 300,000 yuan. The future construction relief is about 600,000 to 1 million yuan. The disaster in Dangtu, Fanchang and other counties is also serious.

▲ Since the establishment of the Flood Relief Association, only a few thousand yuan of relief funds and more than 300 stones of relief rice have been raised and distributed for emergency relief. The emergency relief groups run by other merchants distributed more than 100,000 steamed buns and buns. Now, it has become a situation that is not enough to meet the urgent needs. Yesterday, a special telegram was sent to the Anhui Provincial Government, because the Central Relief Committee has agreed to allocate 170,000 yuan for relief. It is expected that it has been received. Please allocate a few 10,000 yuan first to save people's lives, and then raise funds for construction relief.

▲ Qingshuihe Town, 20 miles away from Wuhu, suddenly had a group of bandits yesterday. Seeing that the whole town was in the flood, all the shops were closed. They planned to abandon it and go elsewhere. There happened to be a Jingxian cargo ship passing through the area, and the bandits opened fire to stop it, boarded the ship to search for plunder. In addition to kidnapping one person, they also shot and injured four shipowners and passengers, including Mei Ronglin, who were sent to Shouzhi Hospital in Wuhu for treatment.

▲ The Wuhu Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Association plans to order all merchants to pay 10% of the registration fee for Japanese goods due to lack of funds. However, those imported after August 10 will be confiscated and destroyed. If it can be implemented, the income will be huge. The merchants have been holding meetings in recent days, and they all said that they would rather close down than admit it. The association also notified the public ticket bureau to not sell tickets for Nisshin Company ships, and ordered the help gangs not to load and unload goods for Japanese ships.

▲ The Wuhu telephone line is rotten and has been broken many times. It is mixed with the electric light line, causing trouble and injury. The County Chamber of Commerce has repeatedly requested the Ministry of Communications to transform it. Recently, the telegraph bureau has received an order from the Ministry of Communications, ordering it to borrow 30,000 yuan from the business community for thorough repair. However, the business community feels it is difficult to raise funds at this time when the flood is so heavy and business is stagnant. (19th)

Songjiang 81

Summary of the Urban Sanitation Meeting: The Urban Sanitation Movement Committee is an organization of party and government agencies. Yesterday (the 19th), the 20th meeting was held to discuss the proposals: (1) How to improve the way cleaning contractors collect feces from residents. It was decided that the Public Security Bureau and the District Office should print leaflets to solicit public opinion from the district residents, and then summarize and consider the opinions after collection. (1) How to regulate the location and cost of building public toilets. It was decided that the location of the public toilets should be based on the survey table, and 11 locations should be selected first. The cost should be about 100 yuan per location. The funds are planned to be offset by the contractor's deposit, and in the future, the feces collected from each public toilet will be accumulated as a return for the deposit. The Bureau and District Council shall submit it to the County Government for record. (1) How to regulate the method of paying for feces. It was decided that the Bureau and the District shall convene the contractors, refer to the previous method of paying, and stipulate the standard of feces fee for the residents in the future, and announce it to all sectors of society, and order the contractors to comply with it.

The Education Bureau asks for rectification of the difficulty in retaining grain for the Education Bureau. The National Tax Collection Office of the Finance Bureau often has the malpractice of retaining and delaying the payment of education surcharges, which has a great impact on the education cause. At the County Government Meeting yesterday, the Education Bureau specially raised this case and asked for rectification methods. It was decided that the Finance Bureau should properly draft rectification methods and submit them for approval.

Changshu 83

The business tax is less than the contract amount. Please reduce it again: The business tax in this county is contracted by the County Chamber of Commerce to the Finance Department for 50,000 yuan, and a collection committee is organized to collect the business tax, which is submitted in four seasons. Unexpectedly, after sending personnel to the countryside to investigate the business tax amount of various merchants in the township, the result was that the assessment was only more than 32,000 yuan, which was 18,000 yuan less than the fixed amount. The association felt difficult to handle, so they convened various trade associations the other day. After discussion, it was proposed that each association should increase the fee and collect more than 4,000 yuan. However, the difference is still more than 10,000 yuan. The Finance Department has not fully paid the summer installment, only paying 8,000 yuan, and there are still 4,500 yuan unpaid. Now it is autumn again, so they sent personnel to Chang to collect the installment. The committee has no way to cope with it. Now it is decided to clear the summer installment first, and then send Commissioner Zhang Shouyi to the province to ask the Finance Department whether it is possible to reduce the tax by 10,000 yuan per year due to the sluggishness of business.

Embezzlement of Education Bureau's Accounting: The Education Bureau of this county has a lot of school land, totaling tens of thousands of mu. The rent collection office hired a chief accountant to specialize in the job of renting land. The position is currently held by Hua Zhaozeng. Hua is the wife's uncle of Wu Jingping, the current director of the accounting department of the Education Bureau. Wu introduced him and has been there for four years. Unexpectedly, this year, a part of the school land was connected to the Finance Bureau's Tax Collection Office for conversion of grain. Unexpectedly, the Tax Collection Office realized that the land was inconsistent, so they told Gao Zishan, the director of the Education Bureau, to conduct a detailed review at the rent collection office, and found out the facts. Not only was the land inconsistent, but also a lot of embezzlement was found in the accounts, so they asked the county to thoroughly investigate and sent the accountant to the county for detention. Now the Education Bureau has hired Pan Xulun, a certified public accountant from Shanghai Lixin, to Chang to liquidate. It is estimated that Hua Zhaozeng's account embezzlement totaled more than 16,000 yuan from the autumn of the 17th year to the spring of the 20th year in two and a half years. Now the Education Bureau has sent the accountant's certificate to the County Government, requesting investigation and handling.

Wuxi 84

The County Government previously received an order from the province to collect additional land tax for grain storage. Due to the heavy flood this year, it was necessary to store more grain quickly to prepare for emergencies. The County Government immediately ordered each district to handle it. Later, it was discussed at the previous district chief meeting. In order to raise funds for grain storage, it was proposed to follow the old precedent and collect additional taxes on silver transport or accept warehouse receipts. The other day, Jiang Zhaoqin, a commissioner from the Department of Civil Affairs, came to Wuxi to inspect the disaster situation and convened a meeting of local agencies to negotiate. It was decided to increase the warehouse fund and collect an additional one dime of silver per mu under the second phase of land tax in the 20th year. Yesterday, the County Government held a County Government Meeting and repeatedly discussed it. It was resolved to submit it to the Department of Civil Affairs and Finance separately and then submit it to the Provincial Government Meeting for approval and implementation.

The dramatic case of robbery in the downtown area: The thief was arrested. Lu Hongtai, a detective from the sixth team of the Second Water Police District, received a secret report yesterday that Wang Xiaomeizi (aka Wang Jinyu), a dramatic thief in the robbery case of Dr. Wang Daoan's house in the downtown area, was hiding outside Guangfu Gate and planned to go to Shanghai to hide. Detective Lu immediately went to arrest him with the police. He was arrested near Qitai Inn and was identified by the informants on the spot. After a detailed interrogation, it was found that he was 31 years old, from Caotang Port, Yancheng, and is now doing small business in Shanghai. In August last year, he robbed a rice shop in Datang Town, Suzhou, with a total of 20 people, carrying eight pistols. After the event, he received 25 yuan. In the case of Wang Daoan's house in the city last month, there were a total of five people, four of whom entered the house, and one was guarding the wind, carrying three pistols. After the event, he received 35 yuan. Now all the accomplices have fled to other counties. He was immediately sent to the District Department and transferred to the county for interrogation.

The series of robbery cases in Kaiyuan Township: Ding Lane, near Meiyuan in the fourth district (Kaiyuan Township) of the county, suddenly came to more than a dozen robbers at 12:00 the other night and robbed two families in a row. They first entered Wang Abao's house, first tied up Abao, and beat him arbitrarily. After searching everywhere, they only got one silver dollar. The robbers shouted bad luck, so they turned to Ding Xishou's house next door and robbed in the same way. The Ding family had some savings, and they were robbed of silver dollars and clothes, worth more than 100 yuan. When the incident happened, a Ding family long-term worker rushed to report to the ninth branch of the Public Security Bureau. When the police were brought to arrest, the thieves were already far away.

The verdict on the Yi Wang case is scheduled to be announced: Yi Ruichang sued Wang Zhichen, the director of the Provincial Hospital, for misconnecting bone joints in the court. The county interrogated the case of conflict between police and broadsword society: In the two townships of Zhouzhuang and Houheng, a farmer, Zhou Dougen, was killed and Xu Bingxiang and Ding Zhuoan were drowned due to a conflict between the two sides related to the capture of bandits. Zhou Dougen was robbed by bandits in the spring. On the 1st of this month, it was reported that Zhang Guangde (leader of the Houheng business group) was suspected of colluding with bandits. After we went to entertain him, we said that it would be better to discuss things. We sent a team of 23 people to search Zhixiang. The other side was all broadsword spears, and they gathered the crowd by beating gongs to resist. We went to the broadsword society's incense hall and were surrounded and opened fire. For self-defense, we fired more than 60 shots, and stray bullets killed Zhou Dougen and others. Hangzhou 88

Measures for the Construction Bureau to Remedy Flood Damage: The Zhejiang Construction Bureau received an order from the Ministry of Industry, stating that this year's floods in various regions are extraordinarily severe, and that many farmlands and crops have been submerged. It ordered guidance for farmers to plant other short-term crops to seek remedies. Now, after investigation, the agricultural crops suitable for autumn planting and that can be harvested in the winter of this year include buckwheat, turnips, radishes, carrots, and others. Those planted in autumn and harvested in the coming spring include wheat, barley, rapeseed, soybeans, and small red beans. Other various grains and crops are mostly not suitable for replanting this year. Regarding the aforementioned short-term autumn crops and spring flowers, the bureau has specially issued orders to county magistrates to widely encourage farmers to seize the time for planting to provide relief, and is also arranging to collect seeds to ensure widespread planting.

Strict Collection of New and Old Taxes: The Zhejiang Provincial Government considers taxes to be the major source of income for the province's treasury, upon which all provincial government expenses depend. The shortfall in subsidies for the 17th, 18th, and 19th years was substantial. Now that the assessment for the 19th year has concluded and the collection of taxes for the 20th year has begun, all new and old taxes must be paid in full within the stipulated time limit. The Finance Bureaus of each county have been ordered to step up collection. Any large households that are hesitant to pay will be strictly pursued without leniency. A special announcement was made yesterday to inform everyone.

Ningbo 89

Private Smugglers Resist Salt Police: The 8th Detachment of the Ningbo Salt Police stationed in Fangmen, Fenghua, dispatched squad leader Chu Anqing and salt police officers Zhang Xiangwei and others on patrol the afternoon before yesterday. At 3 PM, they discovered seven loads of smuggled salt spoken in the Ninghai dialect in the Ge'ao area. They immediately arrested the smugglers. Unexpectedly, while escorting them to the foot of Xiwangwu Mountain beside the creek, at 5 PM, the smugglers put down their loads and, taking advantage of the salt police's unpreparedness, struck Chu Anqing in the back of the head with an iron bar, causing him to faint and placing him in grave danger. The remaining smugglers also used shoulder poles to attack the squad leader, seizing a wooden-cased gun and four rows of bullets, and opened fire. Seeing the situation was unfavorable, the other salt police officers fled in disarray. Salt police officer Zhang Xiangwei fired back in self-defense, killing one smuggler.

Robbery of Letter Delivery Boat Solved: The Quansheng Letter Delivery Bureau boat in front of the Tianhou Palace in Ningbo was robbed of its iron box by bandits on the 15th in the Hemu area south of Xiezhi Mountain within Cixi's jurisdiction. Around 7 PM the night before last, detectives Wu Zhenyuan and others captured two suspects in the case, Xu Kanghai and He Achang, inside a small house at Shengbao Bridge on the north bank of the Jiang River. The lost foreign silver has also been recovered.

Hefei 90

Rice-Snatching Riots Expand: After more than seventy dikes of various sizes along the rivers and lakes were breached by floods, over ten thousand starving refugees are crying out for food. The ignorant, incited by bandits, have resorted to desperate measures, swarming to the Sancha River, Shikou, and Xinhekou areas along the main waterways of the lake and river. Initially, they only snatched rice boats; the Dongwai Shen Gonghe and other firms have already lost over a thousand shi of rice. Subsequently, large numbers of bandits, posing as disaster victims, also searched and robbed boats carrying salt and other goods, causing travelers to hesitate and commerce to cease. Even water bandits are intercepting boats in the middle of the lake. Rice snatching has also spread to Chaoxian's transport routes and other places. Businesses in Hefei have held consecutive meetings in recent days, resolving to send representatives to the county government to request a police squad to escort goods from various firms to Hefei, to ensure safety. They have also sent a letter to the Chaohu Water Police Bureau, urging them to quickly devise relief measures to maintain temporary transportation, and to formulate a lake defense plan for lasting peace. The escort police have already departed for Chaoxian this morning.

Educational News 91

Important News

Implementation Plan for Universally Establishing Agricultural, Medical, and Engineering Vocational Schools in Provinces and Cities (1) 92

The Ministry of Education's "Implementation Plan for Establishing Three Types of Vocational Schools: Agricultural, Medical, and Engineering in Various Provinces and Cities," which was intended to be submitted to the Executive Yuan and then to the National Government, was sent by the National Government to the Central Political Council. The council then handed it over to the Education and Finance Groups for review. The results were that "the length of study for medical vocational schools in the implementation plan should be changed to four years. Also, Hankou City has been changed to a city not directly under the Executive Yuan. In the attached table of the original draft, Hankou City should be relisted in the column for cities with a population of over 300,000." The review report of the two groups has been passed by the 276th Central Political Council according to the review opinions. After receiving the order, the Ministry of Education, because the resolution to change the length of study for medical vocational schools to four years contradicted the vocational school regulations, which stipulated that the length of study for medical vocational schools was three years, with one year of internship after completing the three-year curriculum, and based on the recommendation of the Medical Education Committee, the Ministry of Education requested that the length of study for medical or pharmaceutical vocational schools be set at three years plus one year of internship. After receiving the report, the Ministry of Education has forwarded the aforementioned opinions to the Central Government for review. Once approved, the revised implementation plan will be issued to all provinces and cities for compliance. The revised plan is recorded below:

A. Establishment Methods 93

1. Each province should establish one medical vocational school in the provincial capital and one agricultural vocational school in a suitable location in the province.

2. Henan and Hebei provinces, which have already established provincial agricultural colleges, may postpone the establishment of such agricultural vocational schools, or establish specialized courses in the colleges. The old-system provincial agricultural specialized schools in Jiangxi, Sichuan, Shanxi, and Chahar provinces should be reorganized into agricultural vocational schools.

3. Hebei, which has already established a provincial medical college, may postpone the establishment of such medical vocational schools. The old-system provincial medical specialized schools in Zhejiang and Jiangxi provinces should be reorganized into pharmaceutical or medical vocational schools, respectively.

4. Each city directly under the Executive Yuan should establish one medical vocational school and one industrial vocational school.

5. Each city with a population of over 300,000 should establish one medical vocational school.

6. Each province, except Henan, Hebei, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Sichuan, Shanxi, and Chahar, should raise construction funds of 600,000 yuan in the 20th year to fund the establishment of agricultural and medical vocational schools. The allocation is as follows: (1) Agricultural vocational school: 300,000 yuan for start-up costs (estimated for the establishment of three departments); (2) Medical vocational school: 300,000 yuan for start-up costs.

7. Each city directly under the Executive Yuan should raise construction funds of 500,000 to 700,000 yuan in the 20th year to fund the establishment of medical and engineering vocational schools. The allocation is as follows: (1) Medical vocational school: 300,000 yuan for start-up costs; (2) Industrial vocational school: 200,000 to 400,000 yuan for start-up costs.

8. Each city with a population of over 300,000 should raise construction funds of 300,000 yuan in the 20th year to fund the establishment of medical vocational schools.

9. Henan, Sichuan, Shanxi, and Chahar provinces should each raise construction funds of 400,000 yuan in the 20th year to be used for establishing medical vocational schools, expanding existing agricultural colleges, or reorganizing agricultural vocational schools.

10. Zhejiang Province should raise construction funds of 400,000 yuan in the 20th year to be used for establishing an agricultural vocational school and reorganizing the existing pharmaceutical specialized school.

11. Jiangxi and Hebei provinces should each raise construction funds of 200,000 yuan in the 20th year to be used for expanding existing agricultural colleges or reorganizing agricultural specialized schools, and for expanding existing medical colleges or reorganizing medical specialized schools.

12. Provinces and cities with special circumstances that cannot simultaneously establish three or two types of vocational schools may stagger the establishment by year, depending on the circumstances. However, in the 20th year, at least one type of vocational school must be established.

13. Each province and each city directly under the Executive Yuan, and each city with a population of over 300,000, should formulate detailed plans based on local needs and the current state of education regarding the departments to be established in the aforementioned three types of vocational schools, the location of the schools, and the expenses required, and report them to the Ministry of Education within three months. After approval, preparations should begin, and the establishment should be completed by the 20th year, with classes beginning in the first semester of the 21st year.

B. Establishment Standards 94

1. The establishment standards for agricultural vocational schools are as follows:

(1) The organization of agricultural vocational schools should comply with the organization regulations for vocational schools.

(2) Agricultural vocational schools may establish a single department or several departments as needed by each province. The departmentalization should comply with the provisions of Category B of Article 5 of the Vocational School Regulations.

(3) The length of study for agricultural vocational schools is three years or two years, which should be determined based on the departments established and local needs.

(4) Agricultural vocational schools must be attached to a farm of over 5,000 mu. If a forestry department is established, it must be attached to a forest farm of over 10,000 mu. However, the area of the farm and forest farm may be increased or decreased according to the actual conditions of each province.

(5) The start-up costs and the first year's operating expenses of agricultural vocational schools must meet the following standards: 1. Agronomy, forestry, animal husbandry, and aquaculture departments: at least 100,000 yuan for building and equipment costs per department, and at least 60,000 yuan for the first year's operating expenses, excluding the cost of purchasing farms and forest farms. 2. Veterinary medicine, horticulture, and sericulture departments: at least 80,000 yuan for building and equipment costs per department, and at least 50,000 yuan for the first year's operating expenses, excluding the cost of purchasing farms. The above-mentioned start-up and operating expenses may be increased or decreased according to actual conditions. (2) The establishment standards for medical vocational schools are as follows: 1. The organization of medical vocational schools should comply with the organization law for vocational schools. 2. The length of study for medical vocational schools is four years, followed by one year of internship after completing the study (the Ministry has submitted a request to the Executive Yuan, based on the recommendation of the Medical Education Committee, to change the length of study for medical vocational schools to three years, with one year of internship). 3. Medical vocational schools may establish a medical department or a pharmaceutical department concurrently. Schools that establish both are called pharmaceutical medical schools. 4. Medical vocational schools must be attached to a hospital with at least 200 beds. 5. The start-up costs and the first year's operating expenses of medical vocational schools must meet the following standards:

(1) Medical department: at least 150,000 yuan for building and equipment costs, 100,000 yuan for the first year's operating expenses, and 150,000 yuan for the start-up costs of the attached hospital.

(2) Pharmaceutical department: at least 100,000 yuan for building and equipment costs, and 60,000 yuan for the first year's operating expenses.

(3) The establishment standards for industrial vocational schools are as follows:

1. The organization of industrial vocational schools should comply with the organization law for vocational schools. 2. Industrial vocational schools may establish a single department or several departments concurrently. The departmentalization should be determined according to the needs of each city and should comply with the provisions of Category A of Article 5 of the Vocational School Regulations. 3. The length of study for industrial vocational schools is three years or two years, which should be determined based on the departments established and local needs. 4. Industrial vocational schools must be attached to a factory suitable for student practice. 5. The start-up costs and the first year's operating expenses of industrial vocational schools must meet the following standards: (1) Mining and metallurgy, mechanical engineering, and chemical engineering departments: at least 200,000 yuan for building and equipment costs per department, and at least 100,000 yuan for the first year's operating expenses. (2) Civil engineering, hydraulic engineering, architectural, textile, papermaking, and aircraft manufacturing departments: at least 150,000 yuan for building and equipment costs per department, and 80,000 yuan for the first year's operating expenses. (3) Surveying, dyeing, ceramics, and shipbuilding departments: at least 100,000 yuan for building and equipment costs per department, and at least 80,000 yuan for the first year's operating expenses.

The above-mentioned start-up and operating expenses may be increased or decreased according to actual conditions. (Appendix to be continued)

Ministry of Education's Order to the Guizhou Education Bureau 95

▲Explaining Relief for Disputes over Buddhist Educational Property

The Ministry of Education, based on a report from the Guizhou Education Bureau stating that Buddhist associations in various counties outside the province have been established one after another, intending to dispute educational property, and submitting the association's charter for review, requested methods for relief. The Ministry of Education issued an order stating, "The submitted documents are all noted. Temples should comply with the regulations for supervising temples, promoting religious teachings, and, according to their financial situation, engaging in public welfare or charitable undertakings. They must not use associations to seize property or obstruct educational funds. As for temple properties that have been allocated to educational expenses, since the decision was made earlier, they should be permanently used for educational expenses. If the Buddhist association in the province has any of the above-mentioned situations in the future, the bureau should follow the Ministry's order and the local educational expense guarantee measures to handle them according to the facts. Please comply."

Private Universities Must Not Randomly Establish Specialized, Crash Courses, etc. 96

▲Ministry of Education Orders Yuwen College to Stop Enrolling Specialized Students

The Ministry of Education had previously instructed the education bureaus of various provinces and cities, saying, "Managing universities should focus on enriching content and improving standards as the top priority. However, recently, private universities and colleges often randomly establish specialized, crash courses, etc., in order to attract students, which is prone to creating abuses. Starting from this year, all schools should stop enrolling students in the aforementioned attached departments and courses to prevent abuses. If, in reality, there is a need, specialized courses may be attached in accordance with the provisions of Chapter 5 of the University Regulations, etc., but must first be approved by the Ministry before enrollment is allowed. All bureaus are ordered to instruct all universities and colleges that have been registered and whose boards of directors have been registered to comply." Recently, the Ministry of Education saw reports that the private Yuwen College in Beiping yesterday recruited students for specialized and specialized courses, which contradicts the aforementioned Ministry order. The academy specially telegraphed the Beiping Education Bureau to instruct Yuwen College to stop recruiting students for the courses. The original telegram said, "The Beiping Education Bureau has seen reports that Yuwen College in Beiping, Nanjing, Shanghai, and Liaoning is recruiting new students for specialized and specialized courses. Please comply with the Ministry's Instruction No. 1277 and instruct the college to stop recruiting students for specialized and specialized courses, immediately withdraw the advertisement, and report for record."

Ministry of Education to Appoint Permanent Committee Member for Vocational Education Conference Today 97

The Vocational Education Design Committee convened by the Ministry of Education is scheduled to hold its first meeting at the ministry on September 1. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday, the ministry ordered the appointment of Gu Shusen, Zhu Baoqin, and Dai Yingguan as representatives of the ministry to attend, and designated them as permanent members of the committee. It also ordered the appointment of Weng Zhida and Shen Weixia as secretaries of the committee.

Ministry of Education Explains Membership Procedures for Education Associations 98

The Ministry of Education, based on a report from the Shandong Education Bureau forwarded by the Zhucheng County Magistrate requesting an explanation of the membership procedures for education associations, etc., ordered the bureau, "The report is noted. Anyone who meets one of the qualifications in Article 16 of the Education Association Law and has been approved by the membership qualification review committee of the supervising authority may become a member of the education association. Also, a member who has already joined and has one of the following situations: (1) Only met the qualifications stipulated in Clause 1 or 2 of Article 16 at the time of joining, but has now lost the qualification; (2) An event listed in Article 17 has occurred, they should automatically withdraw from the association, or be ordered to withdraw or be removed by the supervising authority, or be ordered to withdraw or be removed by a resolution of the members' assembly. As for the procedures for dismissing education association staff, they should comply with the provisions of Article 25 of the Education Association Law. All membership withdrawals and staff dismissals should be reported annually in accordance with Article 27 of the Education Association Law. Please note and instruct compliance."

Students from Red Areas in Min Province Staying in the Province 99

▲Education Bureau Orders Schools to Allow Exemption from Tuition and Boarding Fees

Fuzhou Correspondence: In this province, counties ravaged by bandits are reduced to ruins, and the people are destitute. The students who come to the province to study, their hometowns having suffered great calamity, naturally feel life is extremely difficult. If relief is not provided, they will inevitably be unable to study or return home. Yesterday, representatives of students from counties such as Changting, Shanghang, and Jianning staying in the province, Huang Minghe and others, earnestly requested relief from the Education Bureau. The Education Bureau formulated relief measures and issued them to all schools, allowing students from red areas to be exempted from tuition and boarding fees to provide relief. The measures are recorded below:

(1) Students from provincial schools in red areas who are truly unable to afford to study may be exempted from paying tuition and boarding fees for this semester. (2) Students requesting exemption must submit an application form, stating their place of origin and the circumstances of the disaster, and obtain a certificate from two or more civil servants or school teachers in the province, which will be forwarded by the school for record. (3) These measures are limited to students whose origin is Longyan, Yongding, Shanghang, Wuping, Changting, Liancheng, Ninghua, Qingliu, Jianning, Taining, Shiwu, Weile, Chong'an, and other counties truly affected by the red disaster. (4) These measures only apply to provincial schools in this province. (5) The free period is limited to the upper semester of the 20th year. (6) These measures will take effect from the date of promulgation and will be reported for record.

Special Section

This Year’s Vocational Facilities Plan for Shanghai Municipal Middle Schools (Continued) 108

Now, let’s discuss the plans for adding vocational groups to the three municipal middle schools in this city. The first is the Shanghai Municipal Xinlu Normal High School, Normal Department's plan to add an agricultural affairs group and a crafts group. The purpose of the agricultural affairs group is truly: 1. To cultivate rural teachers who can work in the fields, possess agricultural knowledge, and adapt to the rural environment; 2. To cultivate teachers who can engage in practical work and develop labor skills; 3. To cultivate craft talents with specialized training; 4. To cultivate work subject teachers to meet the practical needs of elementary school teaching. As for the curriculum, we have formulated it based on the Ministry of Education's provisional standards for normal school courses and with reference to rural education books. Roughly, the subjects related to the agricultural affairs group include: 1. Agriculture and Practice; 2. Rural Sociology and Practice; 3. Animal Husbandry; 4. Farm Facility Management; 5. Rural Education. In addition to the subjects stipulated by the Ministry of Education, the courses for the crafts group include: 1. Rural Education; 2. Specialty Crafts; 3. Paper Crafts; 4. Bamboo Crafts; 5. Woodworking; 6. Earthwork; 7. Metalwork; 8. Factory Practice. Now, regarding equipment, the school originally had sixty to seventy mu of land, but most of it is mulberry tree gardens. Therefore, in the first year, it is necessary to open up agricultural fields and add the necessary equipment for agricultural affairs and art. At the same time, it is also necessary to build a crafts classroom, and physics and chemistry classrooms, each with a room for handcraft materials, equipment, and instruments and medicines, as well as all the necessary woodworking equipment, at an estimated cost of over seven thousand yuan. As for the equipment for metalwork, it will be added gradually, starting in the second and third years.

The second middle school with vocational facilities is the Municipal Jingye Middle School, which will add a surveying and mapping group to the engineering department. Because Shanghai is a commercial and industrial society, the social need is primarily to cultivate commercial and industrial talents. In the future, graduates of the engineering surveying and mapping group can work as assistants to engineers and managers in engineering. If they want to further their studies, they can also prepare for entering science and engineering departments of universities. As for the curriculum of the engineering surveying and mapping group, in addition to revising it according to the Ministry of Education's high school curriculum standards, subjects related to engineering surveying and mapping will be added, including: 1. Projection Drawing; 2. Architectural Drawing; 3. Perspective Drawing; 4. Materials Science; 5. Building Construction; 6. Architectural Decoration; as well as Surveying Practice. Speaking of equipment, because of financial considerations, we will only select the most needed aspects of surveying and mapping and add them in stages. It is estimated that the first year will require adding: (1) a library classroom dedicated to surveying and mapping practice; (2) forty surveying and mapping drawing boards; (3) drawing tables; (4) four leather tape measures; (5) four 100-meter steel rulers, costing approximately over three thousand yuan. The second year will require continuing to add: (1) ten chains; (2) forty surveying poles; (3) eighty iron pegs; (4) two compasses; (5) four levels; (6) four standard leveling rods; (7) two theodolites, costing approximately six thousand yuan. The third year will require continuing to add two theodolites and two plane table surveying sets, costing approximately four thousand yuan. In the future, it will also be necessary to hire two specialized surveying and mapping teachers to ensure the achievement of professional training. The third vocational facility in a middle school is the addition of a home economics group to the normal department of the Municipal Wuben Girls' Middle School. Its purpose is roughly four points: First, to enhance girls' inherent interest and knowledge in home economics; Second, to practice girls' applicable home management skills; Third, to cultivate diligent home economics talents according to the Ministry of Education's plan; Fourth, to research applicable home economics teaching materials and teaching methods for elementary school labor subjects, and to cultivate home economics teachers. As for the curriculum of the home economics group, in addition to the subjects stipulated by the Ministry of Education, there are also required elective subjects for the home economics group, including: 1. Clothing Cutting and Practice; 2. Food Component Chemistry; 3. Food Cooking; 4. Child Care; 5. Embroidery; 6. Home Decoration; 7. Home Hygiene; 8. Home Economics; 9. Household Management; 10. Home Bookkeeping; 11. Home Chemical Crafts; 12. Home Gardening. As for equipment, the first year requires adding: (1) a home chemical crafts practice room; (2) a medical practice room; (3) an embroidery and sewing practice room; (4) four sewing machines; (5) children's toys and children's sports equipment, estimated to cost over one thousand three hundred yuan. The second year requires continuing to add: (1) a Chinese cooking practice room; (2) a Western cooking practice room; (3) kitchen and dining utensils; (4) banquet utensils; (5) continuing to add two sewing machines, estimated to cost one thousand three hundred and fifty yuan. The third year should add: 1. bedroom utensils, 2. living room utensils, 3. various house decoration utensils, 4. family medicines, 5. food storage utensils, 6. various utensils suitable for children's clothing, food, and housing, 7. child care utensils, 8. a home arrangement practice room, 9. a home chemical crafts practice room, 10. a washing and dyeing practice room, estimated to cost over one thousand seven hundred yuan. The hope for the home economics group is to organize the inherent home economics skills of our country using scientific methods, so that the general public can practically apply them in the future. Finally, what remains to be said is that regarding the Shanghai Education Bureau's promotion of productive education, everyone knows that Shanghai is a major commercial port in East Asia, on which the attention of China and foreign countries is focused. Any action in the administrative aspect is sufficient to influence the whole country. At present, in order to carry out the promotion of productive education, this bureau has spent the efforts of many experts, spent a lot of money and time, and is working towards that aspect with twelve points of sincerity. I think there must be many experts in the country willing to assist and cooperate, and think together, in order to achieve it as soon as possible. However, due to talent and time constraints, this bureau will inevitably have many errors in the future, and it is hoped that everyone will give their utmost guidance (End).

Chairman Chiang Returned to Nanjing Yesterday 109

▲Boarded the train at Zhenru Station

▲Immediately Returned to Jiangxi to Suppress Bandits

Chairman Chiang of the National Government returned to Shanghai from Jiangxi this time to personally escort the coffin of Madam Ni, mother of Soong, for burial, and to meet with Madam Sun Yat-sen, Soong Ching-ling, to discuss important matters. At 9:40 yesterday morning, Chairman Chiang returned to Nanjing by train from Zhenru Station. Chief of Guards Wang Shihe and several guards boarded the train with him. Most of the guards departed from the North Station. Important figures were not notified in advance, so at around 9:00 yesterday morning, Mayor Zhang, Police Chief Chen Xizeng, Bureau Chiefs of the two Railways Guo Chengen, Chief of Staff of the Garrison Command Xu Jinyuan, Aides Jiang Yi and Wang Bailing, Yang Xiaotian, Du Yuesheng, and others were waiting at the North Station. They inquired by telephone at the Chiang residence and learned that Chiang had gone directly to Zhenru Station to board the train. The Bureau Chiefs of the two Railways then dispatched Qian Yanling to accompany and take care of him on the train. Those who had come to see him off then dispersed. When Chairman Chiang went to Zhenru Station, the only people seeing him off were Madam Soong Mei-ling and Soong Tzu-an, and others. At 9:40, when the Shanghai-Nanjing train passed through the station, Chiang boarded the attached flower car to Nanjing. It is reported that Chairman Chiang arrived in Nanjing at 4:25 yesterday afternoon and immediately transferred to Jiangxi to suppress bandits.

Chile Establishes New Legation in Shanghai 110

▲Chargé d'Affaires Baixila Visited Mayor Zhang Yesterday

Regarding the establishment of a new Chilean legation in China, it was originally planned to build it in the capital, but due to problems such as location and construction, which could not be resolved in a short time, it was decided to temporarily rent a building in Shanghai for establishment in order to begin formal diplomatic relations with our country's Ministry of Foreign Affairs as soon as possible. It is learned that Mr. Baixila, the newly appointed Chilean Chargé d'Affaires to China, since taking office, in addition to establishing a temporary office in his residence at the Cathay Hotel on the Bund, has now rented a new building, still under construction, on Route Cohen in the French Concession, near the American School and the Polish Legation, in preparation for establishing the new legation and residence. The house is now mostly completed and will soon be finished. Once the new house is completed, he will move from the temporary office on the Bund into the new house and officially start working. He will then notify all sectors of society by letter. Also, since his arrival in Shanghai, the Chargé d'Affaires has been very busy handling the registration of Chilean nationals in Shanghai and preparing for all matters related to the establishment of the new legation, so he has not had time to visit all sectors of society in Shanghai. Yesterday, Mr. Baixila, with some free time due to less official business, specially accompanied by his secretary, Mr. Ma Tianying, visited the Shanghai Mayor Zhang Yuejun at the Municipal Government on Maple Bridge at 11:00 am. They talked for about half an hour before leaving. It is reported that yesterday was the first visit by the Chargé d'Affaires since his arrival in Shanghai, which is the proper etiquette for diplomats upon taking office.
